<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложа́щийся</a> (2156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложа́щийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ložáščijsja</span>)
</p>

***ложе.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>ло́же</a> (6749)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>ло́же</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lože</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <a href = vnd.unilang:лежать.html>лежа́ть</a>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">łoże</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>ло́же</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóže</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>ло́жа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>ло́жа</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>лож</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bed, couch</li>
<li>riverbed; channel</li>
<li>gunstock</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postélʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">riverbed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русло.html>ру́сло</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rúslo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ложиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a> (2156)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ložítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лечь.html>лечь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lie down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>костьми́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ložítʹsja</b> kostʹmí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall in battle, to do one's damnedest, to go all out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совесть.html>со́весть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ložítʹsja</b> na sóvestʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to weigh on one's conscience</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дрейф.html>дрейф</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic<span class="ib-comma qualifier-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ložítʹsja</b> v drejf</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lie to, to heave to</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:основа.html>осно́ву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ložítʹsja</b> v osnóvu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to underlie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больница.html>больни́цу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ložítʹsja</b> v bolʹnícu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to hospital (to be hospitalised)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ложиться.html>ложи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ložítʹsja</b> spatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go to bed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall, to cover <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of snow, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The imperfective form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (without any prefixes and reflexive suffixes) is considered non-standard in modern Russian; <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:класть.html>класть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> should be used instead.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ложно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ложно</a> (31176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ло́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li>falsely <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a false manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ло́жно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóžno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ло́жный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóžnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><a href = vnd.unilang:наречие.html>Наре́чие</a><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<p>I <i>нареч.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>ло́жный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:качество.html>ка́честв</a>.  
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствовать.html>соотве́тствуя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:истина.html>и́стине</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дучи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибочный.html>оши́бочным</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ненастоящий.html>ненастоя́щим</a>. <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложный.html>Ложно</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:истолковать.html>истолкова́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кты</a>. </span> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>ложь</a> (2898)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лъжь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lŭžĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lъžь</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">лъжь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lŭžĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = tr Latn">lož</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">лэш</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ruthenian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ruthenian language">Old Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложе.html>лож</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lož</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-ocs">lež</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">lež</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">lož</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Polish language">Old Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-opl">łeż</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovincian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovincian language">Slovincian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="zlw-slv">łäž</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">lȃž</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">láž</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">lȅž</i> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">tonal orthography</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>. Has an exact reflex in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lyġe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lie</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lugiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>ложь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ložʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>лжи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>лжи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>лжей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lie, falsehood</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>A lie which is told to deceive someone is a <i><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ложь.html>ложь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></i>. Tall tales told without the malicious intention of deceiving others are <i><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вранье.html>враньё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vranʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вранье.html>враньё</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vranʹjó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***локализация.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:локализация.html>локализа́ция</a> (14258)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локализация.html>локализа́ция</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lokalizácija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локализация.html>локализа́ции</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локализация.html>локализа́ции</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локализация.html>локализа́ций</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>localization (act of localizing)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***локализовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:локализовать.html>локализова́ть</a> (23570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">localiser</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ова́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локализовать.html>локализова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lokalizovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to locate, to allocate, to position
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:локализовать.html>локализова́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:неисправность.html>неиспра́вности</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бки</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lokalizovátʹ</b> neisprávnosti (ošíbki)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to isolate faults (errors)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to localize, to contain
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пожар.html>пожа́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:локализованный.html>локализо́ван</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">požár byl lokalizóvan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the fire was contained</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informatics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to localize</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***локон.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:локон.html>ло́кон</a> (20797)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Locken</i>, plural for <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Locke</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локон.html>ло́кон</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lókon</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локон.html>ло́кона</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локон.html>ло́коны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локон.html>ло́конов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lock, curl, ringlet</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*olkъtь</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*Heh₃l-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>ло́коть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lókotʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>ло́ктя</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>ло́кти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>локте́й</a></b>)

***локтевой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:локтевой.html>локтево́й</a> (28652)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локоть.html>ло́коть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lókotʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ево́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:локтевой.html>локтево́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">loktevój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> elbow; ulnar, anconal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:локтевой.html>локтева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>ко́сть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>loktevája</b> kóstʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ulna</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>elbow</b> bone</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cubit; cubital</li></ol>

***ломаный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломаный.html>ло́маный</a> (15173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-аный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-anyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломаный.html>ло́маный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lómanyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>broken
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломаный.html>ло́маная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:линия.html>ли́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lómanaja línija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">broken line</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломаный.html>ло́маный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lómanyj</b> jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">broken language</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грош.html>гроша</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломаный.html>ло́маного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоит</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">groša lómanovo ne stoit</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> it's not worth a twopence; it's not worth a brass farthing; it's not worth a plugged nickel</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">*ло́ман, *ло́мана, *ло́мано, *ло́маны</span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided due to their similarity to short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

***ломать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a> (2786)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lomátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломать.html>слома́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поломать.html>полома́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to fracture</li>
<li>to quarry (stone)</li>
<li>to rack, to cause to ache</li>
<li>to cause (someone) to lose spirit or will</li></ol>

***ломаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломаться.html>лома́ться</a> (7745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломаться.html>лома́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lomátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломаться.html>слома́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поломаться.html>полома́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to break up, to fracture, to split</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break down (of a device, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to collapse, to fall apart</li>
<li>to crack, to break (of the voice)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pose, to mince, to pretend
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поломаться.html>полома́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polomátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be obstinate, to cause difficulties, to refuse to agree
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломаться.html>лома́лся</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потом.html>пото́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уговорить.html>уговори́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>на́ми</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On dólgo <b>lomálsja</b>, no potóm my jevó ugovoríli pojtí s námi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He was pigheaded for a long time but then we convinced him to come with us.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поломаться.html>полома́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">polomátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломать.html>лома́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The perfective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сломаться.html>слома́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slomátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> refers to one single complete act, while <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поломаться.html>полома́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polomátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> refers to a complete stretch of either multiple acts or a continuous act.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to pose, to mince</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выламываться.html>выла́мываться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vylámyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кривляться.html>кривля́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krivljátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to be obstinate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выламываться.html>выла́мываться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vylámyvatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отнекиваться.html>отне́киваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">otnékivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ломающийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломающийся.html>ломающийся</a> (7745)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***ломить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ломи́ть</a> (13225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lomiti</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ломи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lomítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ло́мит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:столб.html>столбы́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>lómit</b> stolbý</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind breaks the poles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to charge forward, to break through</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ache
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ло́мит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кость.html>ко́сти</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>lómit</b> kósti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his bones ache</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ломи́ться</a> (12091)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломить.html>ломи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lomítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ломи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lomítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><i>(third person only)</i> to be <i>(near to)</i> breaking <i>(with)</i>, to burst <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полок.html>по́лки</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ло́мятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pólki <b>lómjatsja</b> ot knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the shelves are crammed with books</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полок.html>по́лки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:магазин.html>магази́нов</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ло́мятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:товар.html>това́ров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pólki magazínov <b>lómjatsja</b> ot továrov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shop shelves are overladen with goods</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветвь.html>ве́тви</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ло́мятся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плод.html>плодо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vétvi <b>lómjatsja</b> ot plodóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boughs are groaning with fruit</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to force one's way <i>(to, into)</i>, to come in crowds <i>(to)</i>, to flock <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:народ.html>наро́д</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ло́мится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:концерт.html>конце́рт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naród <b>lómitsja</b> na koncért</i> ― <span class="e-translation">people are flocking to the show; the show is packing them in</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ломиться.html>ломи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открытый.html>откры́тую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lomítʹsja</b> v otkrýtuju dverʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(try to) force an open door; try to prove the obvious;  preach to the choir</span></div></dd></dl></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ломкий.html>ломка</a> (24775)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломкий.html>ло́мка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lómka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломкий.html>ло́мки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломкий.html>ло́мки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломкий.html>ло́мок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>breaking</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> withdrawal symptoms (as with drug addicts)</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short feminine singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ломкий.html>ло́мкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lómkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
